module test;
using test::*;
using system::*;

var s = "";

class SMSwitchI1 : StateMachine
{	
	$state_machine
	{
		$state_input A();
		$state_input B();
		
		$state default()
		{
			$switch ()
			{
			case A():
				{
					s = $"$(s)[A]";
				}
			}
			s = $"$(s).";
		}
	}
}

func main():string
{
	var sm = new SMSwitchI1^();
	try
	{
		sm.A();
	}
	catch (ex)
	{
		s = $"$(s)!";
	}
	return s;
}
